range\\n     - Result pushed onto stack\\n   - Result stored in `aResult`\\n\\n### Key Design Patterns\\n\\n1. **Token Array Caching**: Compiled bytecode reused across recalculations\\n2. **Formula Grouping**: Multiple cells with identical formula patterns batched together\\n3. **Lazy Evaluation**: Cells only interpreted when needed (dirty flag)\\n4. **Stack-Based**: RPN evaluation model avoids recursion depth issues\\n5. **Context Pooling**: Thread-safe interpreter contexts for parallel evaluation\\n6. **Circular Reference Detection**: `RecursionHelper` detects and handles cycles\\n7. follows a three-stage pipeline: **Compilation** → **Recalculation Scheduling** → **Interpretation & Execution**.\\n\\n### Stage 1: Formula Compilation (Tokenization)\\n\\n**Files:**\\n- `sc/source/core/tool/compiler.cxx` - Primary Calc compiler\\n- `formula/source/core/api/FormulaCompiler.cxx` - Generic formula compiler\\n\\n**Key Class:** `ScCompiler` in compiler.cxx\\n\\n**Entry Point:** `ScCompiler::CompileString(const OUString& rFormula)`\\n- Parses formula text (e.g., \\\"=SUM(A1:A10)\\\")\\n- Produces `ScTokenArray` (bytecode representation)\\n- Handles operator precedence, function recognition, and cell references\\n- Generates reverse Polish notation (RPN) bytecode\\n\\n**Token Array:** Defined in `include/formula/tokenarray.hxx`\\n- Contains sequence of `FormulaToken` objects\\n- Each token has an opcode (ocPush, ocAdd, ocSum, etc.)\\n- Stores recalculation mode metadata (`ScRecalcMode`)\\n\\n### Stage 2: Recalculation Scheduling\\n\\n**Recalculation Modes** (from `include/formula/tokenarray.hxx`):\\n```cpp\\nenum class ScRecalcMode : sal_uInt8 {\\n    NORMAL         = 0x10,  // Normal recalc on dependency change\\n    ALWAYS         = 0x01,  // Always recalculate (volatile functions)\\n    ONLOAD_MUST    = 0x02,  // Must recalculate after file load\\n    ONLOAD_ONCE    = 0x04,  // Recalculate once after load\\n    ONLOAD_LENIENT = 0x08,  // Lenient recalc after load\\n    FORCED         = 0x20,  // Force recalc even if not visible\\n    ONREFMOVE      = 0x40   // Recalc if referenced cell moved\\n}\\n```\\n\\n**Key Classes & Methods:**\\n\\n1. **ScFormulaCell** (`sc/inc/formulacell.hxx` / `sc/source/core/data/formulacell.cxx`)\\n   - Represents a single cell containing a formula\\n   - Member: `pCode` - pointer to `ScTokenArray`\\n   - Member: `bDirty` - flag indicating cell needs recalculation\\n   - Member: `aResult` - cached formula result (`ScFormulaResult`)\\n   - Member: `mxGroup` - reference to formula group for optimization\\n\\n2. **SetDirty() & SetDirtyVar()** in formulacell.cxx\\n   - Called when cell's dependencies change\\n   - Marks cell for recalculation\\n   - Broadcasts to dependent cells via `SvtListener` mechanism\\n\\n3. **CalcFormulaTree()** in document.cxx\\n   - Main recalculation engine\\n   - Walks formula tree and interprets all dirty cells\\n   - Respects recalculation mode flags\\n\\n### Stage 3: Interpretation & Execution\\n\\n**Primary Interpreter Files:**\\n- `sc/source/core/tool/interpr4.cxx` - Main interpreter with entry point\\n- `sc/source/core/tool/interpr1.cxx` through `interpr8.cxx` - Function implementations\\n- `sc/source/core/inc/interpre.hxx` - Class definition\\n\\n**Execution Flow:**\\n\\n1. **ScFormulaCell::Interpret()**  in formulacell.cxx (line ~1500)\\n   - Entry point called during recalculation cycle\\n   - Handles formula groups (optimized batch execution)\\n   - Manages recursion detection and circular reference handling\\n\\n2. **ScFormulaCell::InterpretTail()** in formulacell.cxx (line ~1885)\\n   - Internal method for single cell interpretation\\n   - Creates `ScInterpreterContext` for execution context\\n   - Instantiates `ScInterpreter` object\\n   - Calls `ScInterpreter::Interpret()`\\n\\n3. **ScInterpreter::Interpret()** in interpr4.cxx (line ~3976)\\n   - Main bytecode interpreter loop\\n   - Iterates through `FormulaTokenIterator aCode` (iterates token array)\\n   - For each token:\\n     - If opcode is `ocPush`: push value onto stack\\n     - Otherwise: execute operation (function call, operator, etc.)\\n   - Stack-based evaluation (Forth-like)\\n   - Handles matrix formulas, jump conditions, error propagation\\n\\n4. **Operation Handlers** - `ScInterpreter::ScXXX()` methods\\n   - **interpr1.cxx**: ScIf, ScChoose, ScSum, ScCount, ScAnd, ScOr, etc.\\n   - **interpr2.cxx**: ScGetActDate, ScInt, ScAbs, ScSin, ScCos, etc.\\n   - **interpr3.cxx**: ScVLookup, ScHLookup, ScMatch, ScIndex, etc.\\n   - **interpr6.cxx**: ScSum, ScCount, ScAverage, ScMin, ScMax, etc.\\n   - **interpr7.cxx**: Statistical functions (ScNorm, ScErf, etc.)\\n\\n5. **Result Storage**\\n   - Result pushed onto internal `ScStack` during interpretation\\n   - Final result stored in `ScFormulaCell::aResult` (type `ScFormulaResult`)\\n   - Result can be double, string, matrix, or error code\\n\\n### Supporting Components\\n\\n**ScInterpreterContext** (`sc/source/core/tool/interpretercontext.cxx` / `sc/inc/interpretercontext.hxx`)\\n- Manages interpreter execution context\\n- Thread-local context pools for parallel evaluation\\n- Maintains formatter, document references, and token caches\\n- Provides `ScInterpreterContextGetterGuard` for safe context access\\n\\n### Example: Evaluating =SUM(A1:A10)\\n\\n1. **Compile Phase**\\n   - `ScCompiler::CompileString(\\\"=SUM(A1:A10)\\\")`\\n   - Produces token array: [ocPush(range A1:A10), ocSum, ocStop]\\n\\n2. **Dirty Flagging**\\n   - Any change to A1:A10 calls `SetDirty()` on dependent cells\\n   - Marks cells with `ScRecalcMode::NORMAL` for recalculation\\n\\n3. **Recalculation**\\n   - `CalcFormulaTree()` finds all dirty formula cells\\n   - Respects recalculation mode: ONLOAD_MUST cells recalc after load, ALWAYS cells recalc every time\\n\\n4. **Interpretation**\\n   - `ScFormulaCell::Interpret()` called\\n   - Creates `ScInterpreter` and calls `Interpret()`\\n   - Reads token array:\\n     - Push A1:A10 range onto stack\\n     - Execute `ocSum` → calls `ScInterpreter::ScSum()`\\n     - Sums all numeric values in range\\n     - Result pushed onto stack\\n   - Result stored in `aResult`\\n\\n### Key Design Patterns\\n\\n1. **Token Array Caching**: Compiled bytecode reused across recalculations\\n2. **Formula Grouping**: Multiple cells with identical formula patterns batched together\\n3. **Lazy Evaluation**: Cells only interpreted when needed (dirty flag)\\n4. **Stack-Based**: RPN evaluation model avoids recursion depth issues\\n5. **Context Pooling**: Thread-safe interpreter contexts for parallel evaluation\\n6. **Circular Reference Detection**: `RecursionHelper` detects and handles cycles\\n7. **Volatile Functions**: Functions like NOW, TODAY, RAND marked ALWAYS to recalc every time\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
